# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# etcd MVCC Compaction and Watch Stream Cancellation

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in etcd-io/etcd that implement MVCC compaction: the compaction schedule (periodic vs revision-based), the compaction of revision indices, the notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision, and the slow watch detection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Overview\\nThe etcd MVCC compaction system consists of three main components: (1) compaction scheduling (periodic vs revision-based), (2) compaction of revision indices and data, and (3) notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision with slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/)\\n\\n### Compactor Interface (compactor.go)\\nDefines the `Compactor` interface with `Run()` and `Stop()` methods. Two implementations exist:\\n\\n### Periodic Compaction (periodic.go)\\nImplements time-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Records revisions at 1/10th of the retention period\\n- **Interval**: Compaction happens every hour for periods \u22651 hour, or every retention period for periods <1 hour\\n- **Algorithm**: Maintains a sliding window of revisions, compacting oldest revision when retention period expires\\n- **Key struct**: `Periodic` with fields `period`, `revs` (revision history), `clock`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable)\\n\\n### Revision-Based Compaction (revision.go)\\nImplements revision count-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Runs every 5 minutes\\n- **Calculation**: Compacts at `current_revision - retention`\\n- **Key struct**: `Revision` with fields `retention`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable), `clock`\\n\\n## Compaction Process (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Core Compaction Flow\\n\\n1. **Initiation** (kvstore.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev)`: Public method that locks the store and calls `compactLockfree()`\\n   - `compactLockfree(rev)`: Acquires write lock, calls `updateCompactRev()`, then `compact()`\\n   - `updateCompactRev(rev)`: Updates `compactMainRev`, persists via `SetScheduledCompact()` to backend\\n   - `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()`: Ensures previous compaction finished before starting new one\\n\\n2. **Index Compaction** (index.go, key_index.go)\\n   - `treeIndex.Compact(rev)`: Iterates all keys, calls `keyIndex.compact()` for each\\n   - `keyIndex.compact(lg, atRev, available)`: Removes versions \u2264 atRev, keeps largest one; removes empty generations\\n   - `doCompact(atRev, available)`: Walks through generations to find which revisions to keep\\n   - `treeIndex.Keep(rev)`: Identifies revisions to preserve during compaction\\n   - **Result**: `keep` map contains all revisions that must be preserved\\n\\n3. **Data Compaction** (kvstore_compaction.go)\\n   - `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)`: Main compaction worker\\n   - **Process**:\\n     1. Compacts kvindex via `Keep()` to get revisions to preserve\\n     2. Iterates through backend key-value store in batches\\n     3. Deletes keys for revisions not in `keep` map\\n     4. Computes hash incrementally via `newKVHasher`\\n     5. Commits batches with sleep interval between them\\n     6. Sets `FinishedCompact` metadata when done\\n   - **Metrics**: Tracks `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n4. **Scheduled Compaction Tracking** (store.go)\\n   - `SetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Writes scheduled revision to backend meta bucket\\n   - `UnsafeSetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Unsafe version for batch transactions\\n   - `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact(tx)`: Reads scheduled compaction revision from backend\\n\\n## Watch Stream Notification (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Watch Stream Architecture\\n\\n1. **Watcher Types** (watchable_store.go, watcher.go, watcher_group.go)\\n   - **Synced watchers**: Keep up with current store revisions, in `synced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Unsynced watchers** (slow watchers): Behind current revision, in `unsynced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Victim watchers**: Blocked on send channel, stored separately for retry\\n\\n2. **Watch Stream Registration** (watchable_store.go:127)\\n   - `watch(key, end, startRev, id, ch, fcs)` creates watcher\\n   - If `startRev > currentRev` or `startRev == 0`: goes to `synced` group\\n   - Otherwise: goes to `unsynced` group, increments `slowWatcherGauge`\\n\\n### Compaction Notification Flow\\n\\n1. **Syncing Unsynced Watchers** (watchable_store.go:346)\\n   - `syncWatchersLoop()`: Runs every 100ms (watchResyncPeriod)\\n   - `syncWatchers(evs)`: Batches up to 512 unsynced watchers\\n   - For each batch:\\n     1. Calls `unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)`\\n     2. `choose()` detects and removes watchers with `minRev < compactionRev`\\n     3. Sends `WatchResponse{CompactRevision: compactionRev}` to compacted watchers\\n     4. Sets `w.compacted = true` and removes from group\\n\\n2. **Compaction Detection** (watcher_group.go:237-266)\\n   - `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)`: Iterates all watchers in group\\n   - For each watcher: if `w.minRev < compactRev`:\\n     - Sends `WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, CompactRevision: compactRev}` to channel\\n     - Sets `w.compacted = true` \\n     - Removes watcher from group\\n   - Handles channel blocking with `default` case to retry later\\n\\n3. **Watch Response During Transactions** (watchable_store_txn.go)\\n   - `watchableStoreTxnWrite.End()` calls `notify(rev, evs)` under lock\\n   - Sends normal events only to synced watchers\\n   - Blocked watchers become victims and are retried by `syncVictimsLoop()`\\n\\n### Watch Progress Notification\\n\\n1. **Progress Tracking** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - `progressIfSync(watchers, responseWatchID)`: Sends progress notifications when all watchers synced\\n   - `progress(w)`: Requests progress for specific watcher\\n   - `progressAll(watchers)`: Broadcasts progress to all watchers\\n   - Sent as empty WatchResponse with only revision set\\n\\n2. **Progress Interval** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - Configurable via `WatchProgressNotifyInterval` flag\\n   - Minimum 100ms, default 10 minutes\\n   - Allows clients to track server progress even without events\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n1. **Metrics** (metrics.go)\\n   - `slowWatcherGauge`: Prometheus gauge tracking number of unsynced (slow) watchers\\n   - Victims in separate `victims` list (watcherBatch)\\n   - Retried every 10ms if any victims exist\\n\\n## Related Components\\n\\n1. **Hash Computation** (hash.go)\\n   - `KeyValueHash`: Contains hash, revision, and compactRevision fields\\n   - Incremental hash calculation during compaction via `newKVHasher`\\n   - Allows corruption detection across cluster members\\n\\n2. **API** (server/etcdserver/v3_server.go)\\n   - `Compact(ctx, request)`: RPC handler for explicit compaction requests\\n   - Calls store `Compact()` method with requested revision\\n   - Supports `Physical` flag for synchronous completion\\n\\n3. **KV Interface** (kv.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev) (<-chan struct{}, error)`: Asynchronous compaction with channel for completion signal\\n   - Part of MVCC KV store interface\\n\\n## Key Data Structures\\n\\n- **watchableStore**: Contains `synced` and `unsynced` watcherGroups, `victims` list\\n- **watcherGroup**: Organizes watchers by key ranges using interval trees, enables efficient notification\\n- **watcher**: Individual watch with `minRev`, `startRev`, channel, filter functions, and `compacted` flag\\n- **Revision**: Struct with Main and Sub fields for comparing versions\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nEtcd's MVCC compaction is a sophisticated system that:\\n1. Schedules compaction either periodically (time-based) or by revision count\\n2. Performs index and data compaction in batches with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n3. Notifies watch streams of compaction via separate handling in watcher groups\\n4. Detects and tracks slow (unsynced) watchers separately from synced ones\\n5. Overview\\nThe etcd MVCC compaction system consists of three main components: (1) compaction scheduling (periodic vs revision-based), (2) compaction of revision indices and data, and (3) notification of watch streams that span a compacted revision with slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/)\\n\\n### Compactor Interface (compactor.go)\\nDefines the `Compactor` interface with `Run()` and `Stop()` methods. Two implementations exist:\\n\\n### Periodic Compaction (periodic.go)\\nImplements time-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Records revisions at 1/10th of the retention period\\n- **Interval**: Compaction happens every hour for periods \u22651 hour, or every retention period for periods <1 hour\\n- **Algorithm**: Maintains a sliding window of revisions, compacting oldest revision when retention period expires\\n- **Key struct**: `Periodic` with fields `period`, `revs` (revision history), `clock`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable)\\n\\n### Revision-Based Compaction (revision.go)\\nImplements revision count-based retention:\\n- **Schedule**: Runs every 5 minutes\\n- **Calculation**: Compacts at `current_revision - retention`\\n- **Key struct**: `Revision` with fields `retention`, `rg` (RevGetter), `c` (Compactable), `clock`\\n\\n## Compaction Process (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Core Compaction Flow\\n\\n1. **Initiation** (kvstore.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev)`: Public method that locks the store and calls `compactLockfree()`\\n   - `compactLockfree(rev)`: Acquires write lock, calls `updateCompactRev()`, then `compact()`\\n   - `updateCompactRev(rev)`: Updates `compactMainRev`, persists via `SetScheduledCompact()` to backend\\n   - `checkPrevCompactionCompleted()`: Ensures previous compaction finished before starting new one\\n\\n2. **Index Compaction** (index.go, key_index.go)\\n   - `treeIndex.Compact(rev)`: Iterates all keys, calls `keyIndex.compact()` for each\\n   - `keyIndex.compact(lg, atRev, available)`: Removes versions \u2264 atRev, keeps largest one; removes empty generations\\n   - `doCompact(atRev, available)`: Walks through generations to find which revisions to keep\\n   - `treeIndex.Keep(rev)`: Identifies revisions to preserve during compaction\\n   - **Result**: `keep` map contains all revisions that must be preserved\\n\\n3. **Data Compaction** (kvstore_compaction.go)\\n   - `scheduleCompaction(compactMainRev, prevCompactRev)`: Main compaction worker\\n   - **Process**:\\n     1. Compacts kvindex via `Keep()` to get revisions to preserve\\n     2. Iterates through backend key-value store in batches\\n     3. Deletes keys for revisions not in `keep` map\\n     4. Computes hash incrementally via `newKVHasher`\\n     5. Commits batches with sleep interval between them\\n     6. Sets `FinishedCompact` metadata when done\\n   - **Metrics**: Tracks `indexCompactionPauseMs`, `dbCompactionTotalMs`, `dbCompactionKeysCounter`, `dbCompactionLast`\\n\\n4. **Scheduled Compaction Tracking** (store.go)\\n   - `SetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Writes scheduled revision to backend meta bucket\\n   - `UnsafeSetScheduledCompact(tx, value)`: Unsafe version for batch transactions\\n   - `UnsafeReadScheduledCompact(tx)`: Reads scheduled compaction revision from backend\\n\\n## Watch Stream Notification (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n### Watch Stream Architecture\\n\\n1. **Watcher Types** (watchable_store.go, watcher.go, watcher_group.go)\\n   - **Synced watchers**: Keep up with current store revisions, in `synced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Unsynced watchers** (slow watchers): Behind current revision, in `unsynced` watcherGroup\\n   - **Victim watchers**: Blocked on send channel, stored separately for retry\\n\\n2. **Watch Stream Registration** (watchable_store.go:127)\\n   - `watch(key, end, startRev, id, ch, fcs)` creates watcher\\n   - If `startRev > currentRev` or `startRev == 0`: goes to `synced` group\\n   - Otherwise: goes to `unsynced` group, increments `slowWatcherGauge`\\n\\n### Compaction Notification Flow\\n\\n1. **Syncing Unsynced Watchers** (watchable_store.go:346)\\n   - `syncWatchersLoop()`: Runs every 100ms (watchResyncPeriod)\\n   - `syncWatchers(evs)`: Batches up to 512 unsynced watchers\\n   - For each batch:\\n     1. Calls `unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)`\\n     2. `choose()` detects and removes watchers with `minRev < compactionRev`\\n     3. Sends `WatchResponse{CompactRevision: compactionRev}` to compacted watchers\\n     4. Sets `w.compacted = true` and removes from group\\n\\n2. **Compaction Detection** (watcher_group.go:237-266)\\n   - `chooseAll(curRev, compactRev)`: Iterates all watchers in group\\n   - For each watcher: if `w.minRev < compactRev`:\\n     - Sends `WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, CompactRevision: compactRev}` to channel\\n     - Sets `w.compacted = true` \\n     - Removes watcher from group\\n   - Handles channel blocking with `default` case to retry later\\n\\n3. **Watch Response During Transactions** (watchable_store_txn.go)\\n   - `watchableStoreTxnWrite.End()` calls `notify(rev, evs)` under lock\\n   - Sends normal events only to synced watchers\\n   - Blocked watchers become victims and are retried by `syncVictimsLoop()`\\n\\n### Watch Progress Notification\\n\\n1. **Progress Tracking** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - `progressIfSync(watchers, responseWatchID)`: Sends progress notifications when all watchers synced\\n   - `progress(w)`: Requests progress for specific watcher\\n   - `progressAll(watchers)`: Broadcasts progress to all watchers\\n   - Sent as empty WatchResponse with only revision set\\n\\n2. **Progress Interval** (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go)\\n   - Configurable via `WatchProgressNotifyInterval` flag\\n   - Minimum 100ms, default 10 minutes\\n   - Allows clients to track server progress even without events\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection (server/storage/mvcc/)\\n\\n1. **Metrics** (metrics.go)\\n   - `slowWatcherGauge`: Prometheus gauge tracking number of unsynced (slow) watchers\\n   - Incremented when watcher added to `unsynced` group (line 148 in watchable_store.go)\\n   - Decremented when moved to `synced` or when victim processing completes\\n   - Set from victim batch size in `syncWatchers()` (line 411)\\n\\n2. **Slow Watcher Identification**\\n   - Any watcher with `minRev < currentRev` at creation time\\n   - Any watcher that becomes blocked on send channel (becomes victim)\\n   - Separate tracking in `unsynced` watcherGroup distinct from `synced`\\n   - `maxWatchersPerSync = 512`: Limits batch size for fairness\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing** (watchable_store.go:257-339)\\n   - `syncVictimsLoop()`: Continuously retries blocked watchers\\n   - `moveVictims()`: Attempts to send queued responses again\\n   - Victims in separate `victims` list (watcherBatch)\\n   - Retried every 10ms if any victims exist\\n\\n## Related Components\\n\\n1. **Hash Computation** (hash.go)\\n   - `KeyValueHash`: Contains hash, revision, and compactRevision fields\\n   - Incremental hash calculation during compaction via `newKVHasher`\\n   - Allows corruption detection across cluster members\\n\\n2. **API** (server/etcdserver/v3_server.go)\\n   - `Compact(ctx, request)`: RPC handler for explicit compaction requests\\n   - Calls store `Compact()` method with requested revision\\n   - Supports `Physical` flag for synchronous completion\\n\\n3. **KV Interface** (kv.go)\\n   - `Compact(trace, rev) (<-chan struct{}, error)`: Asynchronous compaction with channel for completion signal\\n   - Part of MVCC KV store interface\\n\\n## Key Data Structures\\n\\n- **watchableStore**: Contains `synced` and `unsynced` watcherGroups, `victims` list\\n- **watcherGroup**: Organizes watchers by key ranges using interval trees, enables efficient notification\\n- **watcher**: Individual watch with `minRev`, `startRev`, channel, filter functions, and `compacted` flag\\n- **Revision**: Struct with Main and Sub fields for comparing versions\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nEtcd's MVCC compaction is a sophisticated system that:\\n1. Schedules compaction either periodically (time-based) or by revision count\\n2. Performs index and data compaction in batches with sleep intervals to avoid blocking\\n3. Notifies watch streams of compaction via separate handling in watcher groups\\n4. Detects and tracks slow (unsynced) watchers separately from synced ones\\n5. Implements victim/retry pattern for blocked watchers\\n6. Provides progress notifications to allow clients to stay informed of server progress\\n\"\n}\n",
